name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in August 2022
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:3.5
posted:Posted August 25, 2022
msg:I would definitely stay here again.  However, I have stayed at other great hotels in Qingdao and by comparison:
- The location is very average.  The "mall" next door is ok to visit but nothing like its counterparts (ie: Gold Lion Mall near Hyatt, MixC mall next to Shangrila and Westin)
- Cleanliness is great, although small details are missed unlike at a 5 star hotel.  
- The cleaning lady was very sweet and very courteous to us and was available to clean whenever we left for a few hours during the day.  Service was also good, but fell a bit short of other hotels I've stayed at. 
- Facilities seemed average although I did not get to explore much.  
In the room we stayed in, you could also hear this periodic high frequency humming noise which I think came from the HVAC fans that you can see on top of the Big Thumbs mall (Â§ßÊãáÊåá) right outside our room.  After a while, it just became white noise to me but my wife is a light sleeper so she was not that fond of it.  

Overall, I have no major complaints about the Himalaya hotel.  Actually, one thing that I should point out is that the price per night was about $100-$200 less than the hotels I normally stay at in Qingdao (ie: Hyatt, Shangrila).  So if you factor in the significantly lower price, all my ratings above would have gone up one more star.  Again, I would definitely stay here again for the right price and if the hotels I normally stay at are $200-$300 per night during tourist seasons.
